***mijmeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijmeren.html>mijmeren</a> (68729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mimeren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mīmrōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mīmrōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to think, have in mind, care for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mer-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*smer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall into thought, remember, care for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mimorian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember, keep in mind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">remember</span>.
</p>

***mijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> (36)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mīnaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijne.html>mijne</a></b>, <i>contracted form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">m'n</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>belonging to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>: my
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>my</b> mine.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame" style="float: left; width: 65em">
<div class="NavHead" style="background: CCCCFF;">Dutch personal pronouns</div>
<div class="NavContent">

</div></div>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mina.html>mina</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mēnis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ore, metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Some senses are borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">explosive device</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">mine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:tunnel.html>tunnel</a> for sapping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijnen.html>mijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">mijntje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mine</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">place where ore <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> out of the ground</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:delven.html>delven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <b>mine</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> my <b>mine</b>, go excavate somewhere else.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mine</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">device meant to explode when stepped upon or <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opblazen.html>opblazen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <b>mine</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> my <b>mine</b>, go blow yourself up somewhere else.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mine</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:tunnel.html>tunnel</a> used for sapping enemy defence works or lines</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shaft dug by an insect larva in plant <a href = vnd.unilang:organs.html>organs</a>, such as leaves</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mijnre</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijnen.html>mijnen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to buy at an auction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> noun <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijner.html>mijner</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">mijners</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> buyer or bidder at a public auction
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bieder.html>bieder</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijnen.html>mijnen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> noun <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mīta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mītōn</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mēta</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mikken.html>mikken</a> (12152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">micken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mikken.html>mikken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mikjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mikken.html>mikken</a></strong>
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to intend</li></ol>

***milieu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a> (7943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:milieus.html>milieus</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieutje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>environment
<ul><li><b>2006</b>, Hilde Greefs, <i>Water Management, Communities, and Environment: The Low Countries in Comparative Perspective, C. 1000 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> C. 1800</i>, Academia Press, pages 195:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> turfwinning <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onbedoeld.html>onbedoeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolg.html>gevolg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a></b>: bodemdaling <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> -erosie <a href = vnd.unilang:waardoor.html>waardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> waterbeheer <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:problematisch.html>problematisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:karakter.html>karakter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kreeg.html>kreeg</a>.
<dl><dd>But peat extraction <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> an unintended consequence for the <b>environment</b>: sinking and erosion of the soil which made water management problematic in character.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a></a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Mallet-Stevens <a href = vnd.unilang:stamde.html>stamde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegoed.html>gegoed</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mallet-Stevens <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> from a well-off <b>family</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:milieu.html>milieu</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:sociologie.html>sociologie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sociale.html>sociale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omgeving.html>omgeving</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:maatschappelijk.html>maatschappelijk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:cultureel.html>cultureel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:religieus.html>religieus</a>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:militie.html>militie</a> (12531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">milice</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">militia</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Military personnel.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

***min.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a> (2806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:minne.html>minne</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">minnemoeder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minnen.html>minnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minnetje.html>minnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wetnurse</li>
<li>maid, especially a nursemaid</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">minnemoeder</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>minus
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">minus</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Comparative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a></i></span>; less, fewer.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_4">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minst.html>minst</a></b>)

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>min</a></strong>

***minder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a> (670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">minre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">minniro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*minnizô</i>, comparative of adjective deriving from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*minu-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">comparative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a></i></span></span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en">less</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fewer</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">comparative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a></i></span></span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en">less</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">worse</span>, not as <span class="Latn" lang="en">good</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardappelen.html>aardappelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heerlijk.html>heerlijk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biefstuk.html>biefstuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The potatoes <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> delicious, but the <a href = vnd.unilang:steak.html>steak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>not as good</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>less fortunate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijd.html>wedstrijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewonnen.html>gewonnen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkel.html>enkel</a> verzwikt, <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a> the competition, but I <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> sprain my ankle, so that's <b>less fortunate</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span> “klein” in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:benaming.html>benaming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:intervallen.html>intervallen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:akkoorden.html>akkoorden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toonladders.html>toonladders</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoemd.html>genoemd</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:combinatie.html>combinatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> terts-interval
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terts.html>terts</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> interval <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>: “groot”,  “klein” (<b><a href = vnd.unilang:mineur.html>mineur</a></b>), “overmatig” of “verminderd” <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> kleinetertstoonladder, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b>mineurtoonladder</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derde.html>derde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> “kleine <a href = vnd.unilang:terts.html>terts</a>.”</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:akkoord.html>akkoord</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b>mineurakkoord</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minimaal.html>minimaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> interval “kleine <a href = vnd.unilang:terts.html>terts</a>.”</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ming.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ming.html>ming</a> (14531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mingen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mengen.html>mengen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mengan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix, combine, unite, associate with, consort, cohabit with, disturb, converse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mangijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix, knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*menk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rumple, knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mengen.html>mengen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix, blend, mingle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:mengen.html>mengen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">mænge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġemang</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mixture, union, troop, crowd, multitude, congregation, assembly, business, cohabitation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">among</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ming.html>ming</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mings</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">minging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">minged</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">meint</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>ment</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mix, blend, mingle.
<ul><li><b>1562</b>, William Turner, <i>Baths</i>:
<dl><dd>I founde here and there litle peces of marquesites and stones, <b>menged</b> with copper, but I could by no sense or <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> perceyue, that the bathes <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> any notable qualitie thereof.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To bring (people, animals etc.) together; to be joined, in marriage or sexual intercourse.
<ul><li><b>1590</b>, Edmund Spenser, <i>The Faerie Queene</i>, I.ii:
<dl><dd>the old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> [...] him <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> into a secret part, / Where that false couple <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> full closely <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>ment</a></b> / In wanton <a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a> and lewd embracement [...].</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To produce through mixing; especially, to knead.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to mix</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bemingle</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">combine</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mang</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">meddle</span>; see also Thesaurus:mix</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to have sex</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">do it</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">get it on</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">meddle</span>; see also Thesaurus:copulate</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ming.html>ming</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Mixture.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Backformation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">minging</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ming.html>ming</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mings</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">minging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">minged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be unattractive (person or object).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be foul-smelling.</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mingen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mengen.html>mengen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mungen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">muneȝen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">myngian</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mynegian</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġemynegian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring to mind, have in mind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">myne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġemunan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*munaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to think</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*men-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to think</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Merged in Middle English with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġemyndgian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember, be mindful, remind, intend, commemorate, mention, exhort, impel, warn, demand payment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">mind</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ming.html>ming</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mings</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">minging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">minged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To speak of; mention; tell; relate.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To speak; tell; talk; discourse.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:miniatuur.html>miniatuur</a> (34027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from Medieval <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">miniatura</i>.

</p>
